AI prompt-based content generation (server-side)\n- dynamic-content - Placeholder for server-side dynamic content\n\n**Atomic Wind (Primitive Tailwind-based components - experimental)**\n- atomic-wind/box - BLOCK PATTERNS & TEMPLATES\n\n**Pattern Library:**\n- **60+ pre-built patterns** in `/inc/patterns/` covering:\n  - **Business Pack:** homepage, about, contact, services\n  - **Fitness Pack:** homepage, about, contact, groups\n  - **Creator Pack:** (implied from categories)\n  - **Recipes Pack:** (implied from categories)\n  - **Call-to-Action:** 7 variations\n  - **Features:** 5 variations\n  - **Testimonials:** 3 variations + centered, inline image variants\n  - **Forms:** 4 variations\n  - **Pricing:** standard table pattern\n  - **Team:** 2 variations\n  - **Hero sections:** 2 + area-with-button variant\n  - **Gallery:** masonry gallery\n  - **Countdown:** pre-configured countdown pattern\n  - **FAQ:** accordion pattern (implied)\n\n**Pattern Registration:**\nFile: `/Users/varundubey/Local Sites/mediaverse/app/public/wp-content/plugins/otter-blocks/inc/class-patterns.php`\n\n- 12 block pattern categories registered via `register_block_pattern_category()`\n- Patterns stored as PHP files with `<!-- wp:otter-blocks/... -->` markup\n- Minimum WordPress version specified per pattern (e.g., 5.8, 5.9)\n- Full page templates (Pages category) for complete site builders\n\nExample pattern names: `hero-area-with-button`, `content-with-progress-bars`, `contact-details-and-form`, `testimonial-columns`\n\n---\n\n### 3. SHARED ARCHITECTURE\n\n**Editor Components & Controls:**\n\n**Responsive Control Pattern:**\nEvery sizing/spacing attribute follows Desktop → Tablet → Mobile naming:\n- `propertyName` (desktop)\n- `propertyNameTablet`\n- `propertyNameMobile`\n\nExamples from advanced-columns block.json:\n```json\n\"columnsWidthTablet\": {\"type\": \"string\"},\n\"columnsWidthMobile\": {\"type\": \"string\"},\n\"paddingTablet\": {\"type\": \"object\"},\n\"paddingMobile\": {\"type\": \"object\"}\n```\n\n**Shared Styling Attributes (all blocks support):**\n- `backgroundColor`, `color`, `linkColor`, `colorHover`\n- `backgroundType` (color | image | gradient)\n- `borderColor`, `borderWidth`, `borderStyle`, `borderRadius`\n- `padding` / `paddingTablet` / `paddingMobile` (object with top/right/bottom/left)\n- `margin` / `marginTablet` / `marginMobile`\n- `boxShadow` (object-based control)\n- `isSynced` (array of property names synced to global defaults)\n\n**CSS Variable System:**\nBlocks use CSS custom properties prefixed with `--`:\n- `--text-color`, `--link-color`, `--content-color-hover`\n- `--background`, `--border-color`, `--border-radius`\n- `--padding`, `--margin`, `--gap`, `--height`, `--width`\n\nFile: `/Users/varundubey/Local Sites/mediaverse/app/public/wp-content/plugins/otter-blocks/inc/css/blocks/class-shared-css.php`\n\n**Box Control Pattern:**\nFrom CSS_Utility class, all box-like properties use:\n```php\narray(\n  'left' => 'value',\n  'right' => 'value',\n  'top' => 'value',\n  'bottom' => 'value'\n)\n```\n\nHelper methods:\n- `CSS_Utility::box_values()` - Convert object to CSS string\n- `CSS_Utility::make_box()` - Create uniform box\n- `CSS_Utility::merge_views()` - Merge desktop/tablet/mobile boxes\n\n---\n\n### 4. CSS ARCHITECTURE\n\n**Frontend CSS Output System:**\n\n**Architecture:** Per-block CSS generation + global deduplication\n- CSS generated on post save (REST API)\n- Inline styles in `<style id=\"wp-block-ID\">` tags in footer\n- Minified using `tubalmartin\\CssMin\\Minifier`\n\n**CSS Generation Flow:**\n\n1. **CSS_Utility** (`class-css-utility.php`)\n   - Universal CSS generator supporting media queries\n   - Pattern-based value substitution\n   - Conditional property rendering\n   - Global CSS variable sync\n\n2. **Block-Specific CSS Classes** \n   Each block has dedicated CSS class in `/inc/css/blocks/class-{blockname}-css.php`:\n   - Accordion_CSS, Button_CSS, Countdown_CSS, Form_CSS, Popup_CSS, Posts_CSS, etc.\n   - Extends Base_CSS\n   - Implements `render_css($block)` method\n\n3. **Shared CSS Handler**\n   File: `/Users/varundubey/Local Sites/mediaverse/app/public/wp-content/plugins/otter-blocks/inc/css/class-shared-css.php`\n   - Common patterns applied to all blocks\n   - Background layers (color, image, gradient with position/repeat/attachment/size)\n   - Responsive text color, link color\n   - Overlay effects with blend modes\n\n4. **Frontend CSS Enqueuing**\n   File: `/Users/varundubey/Local Sites/mediaverse/app/public/wp-content/plugins/otter-blocks/inc/css/class-block-frontend.php`\n   - Google Fonts enqueued per post (post_meta: `_themeisle_gutenberg_block_fonts`)\n   - Widget CSS enqueued in footer\n   - FSE (Full Site Editing) CSS support\n\n**CSS Variable System:**\n\nAll blocks output CSS variables that can be overridden:\n```css\n#wp-block-id {\n  --text-color: #333;\n  --background: linear-gradient(...);\n  --border-radius: 4px;\n  --padding: 20px 30px 20px 30px;\n}\n```\n\n**Theme Isolation:**\n- Block-level ID prefixed selectors prevent global style pollution\n- `.wp-block-themeisle-blocks-{blockname}` auto-applied\n- Custom CSS selectors via `selector` parameter in CSS_Utility\n\n**Media Query System:**\n```php\n$default_queries = array(\n  'desktop' => '@media ( min-width: 960px )',\n  'tablet'  => '@media ( max-width: 960px )',\n  'mobile'  => '@media ( max-width: 768px )' // inferred\n);\n```\n\nBreakpoints: Desktop (960px+), Tablet (768-960px), Mobile (<768px)\n\n---\n\n### 5. ADVANCED FEATURES\n\n**Box Shadow Implementation:**\n\nStandard object structure across all blocks:\n```json\n\"boxShadow\": {\n  \"type\": \"object\",\n  \"default\": {\n    \"active\": false,\n    \"colorOpacity\": 50,\n    \"blur\": 5,\n    \"spread\": 1,\n    \"horizontal\": 0,\n    \"vertical\": 0\n  }\n}\n```\n\nFiles with shadow controls: Accordion, Advanced Columns, Button, Flip, Popup, Posts Grid, Review, etc.\n\nUsage in CSS: `box-shadow: Xpx Ypx Bpx Spx rgba(Color, Opacity/100);`\n\n**Countdown Timer Expire Actions:**\nFile: `/Users/varundubey/Local Sites/mediaverse/app/public/wp-content/plugins/otter-blocks/build/blocks/countdown/block.json`\n\nAttributes:\n- `onEndAction` (string) - Action when timer expires\n  - Implied values: \"redirect\", \"hide\", \"show\" (based on redirectLink attribute)\n- `redirectLink` (string) - URL to redirect to on expire\n- `behaviour` (string) - Timer behavior mode\n- `mode` (string) - Display mode (days/hours/minutes/seconds)\n- `timer` (object) - Timer configuration\n- `startInterval` / `endInterval` (strings) - Recurring timer bounds\n\n**Visibility Conditions System:**\nFile: `/Users/varundubey/Local Sites/mediaverse/app/public/wp-content/plugins/otter-blocks/inc/plugins/class-block-conditions.php`\n\n- Attribute: `otterConditions` (array) added to ALL blocks dynamically\n- Conditions evaluated on frontend render via `render_blocks()` filter\n- Collection-based logic: multiple condition groups OR'd together\n- Each group: multiple conditions AND'd together\n- Supports: user role, user logged-in, post type, custom post type, device type (mobile/tablet/desktop), date/time range\n\nReturns empty string if conditions unmet (hiding the block).\n\n**Animation Controls:**\nFile: `/Users/varundubey/Local Sites/mediaverse/app/public/wp-content/plugins/otter-blocks/inc/class-blocks-animation.php`\n\nSupported animations:\n- Count animation (number counter)\n- Typing animation\n- General animation framework for AMP compatibility\n\nTriggers: hover, scroll, click, auto-play\n\nEnqueued scripts:\n- `otter-animation` (main animation JS)\n- `anim-count` (counter animation)\n- `anim-typing` (typing animation)\n\n**Dynamic Content & Magic Tags:**\nFile: `/Users/varundubey/Local Sites/mediaverse/app/public/wp-content/plugins/otter-blocks/inc/plugins/class-dynamic-content.php`\n\n**Custom Tags (rendered on frontend):**\n- `<o-dynamic>` - Post/term/user field with filters\n  - Attributes: `data-type`, `data-id`, `data-before`, `data-after`, `data-length`, `data-date-type`, `data-date-format`, `data-date-custom`, `data-time-type`, `data-time-format`, `data-time-custom`, `data-term-type`, `data-term-separator`, `data-meta-key`, `data-parameter`, `data-format`, `data-context`, `data-taxonomy`\n  \n- `{otterDynamic?...}` - Magic tag syntax with same parameters\n\n- `<o-dynamic-link>` - Dynamic URL generation\n  - Attributes: `data-type`, `data-target`, `data-meta-key`, `data-context`\n\n- `<o-dynamic-image>` - Dynamic image URL\n  - Filters images before output\n\n**WooCommerce Integration Blocks:**\n\n1. **Stripe Checkout Block**\n   - Direct payment collection\n   - Product/price configuration\n   - Success/cancel messages\n   - Autoresponder integration\n\n2. **Form Stripe Field**\n   - Nested in Form block\n   - Product picker integration\n   - Ancestor: themeisle-blocks/form\n\n3. **Review Block**\n   - Star ratings (individual features + overall)\n   - Product details (price, discounted price)\n   - Pros/cons lists\n   - Affiliate links with sponsored badge\n   - Currency formatting\n\n**Email Integration Providers:**\nFiles: `/inc/integrations/providers/`\n\n1. **Mailchimp** (`class-mailchimp.php`)\n   - List fetching via API\n   - Contact subscription\n   - Double opt-in support\n   - Field mapping\n\n2. **Sendinblue** (`class-sendinblue.php`)\n   - Alternative to Mailchimp\n   - Same integration pattern\n\n**Form Server-Side Processing:**\nFile: `/inc/server/class-form-server.php`\n\n- Email delivery via `wp_mail()`\n- Provider subscription (Mailchimp/Sendinblue)\n- reCAPTCHA validation\n- File upload handling\n- Nonce verification\n- Custom action hooks for extensions\n- Redirect on submission\n- Response messages\n\n---\n\n### 6. UNIQUE PATTERNS WORTH ADOPTING\n\n**Innovative Architecture Decisions:**\n\n**1. CSS_Utility Pattern Matcher**\n```php\n'property'       => 'margin',\n'pattern'        => 'top right bottom left',\n'pattern_values' => [\n  'top' => ['value' => 'marginTop', 'unit' => 'px'],\n  'right' => ['value' => 'marginRight', 'unit' => 'px'],\n  // ...\n]\n```\n- Powerful abstraction for generating CSS from block attributes\n- Enables complex patterns without manual CSS concatenation\n- Fully conditional with `condition` callbacks\n\nFile: `/Users/varundubey/Local Sites/mediaverse/app/public/wp-content/plugins/otter-blocks/inc/css/class-css-utility.php` (lines 250-304)\n\n**2. Global Sync System (isSynced)**\n- Array of property names marking which attributes use global theme values\n- Stored in block attributes for persistence\n- CSS generation checks `isSynced` array and outputs `var(--global-name)` instead of inline values\n- Enables theme switching without block editing\n\nCode pattern:\n```php\nif ( isset( $attrs['isSynced'] ) && in_array( 'backgroundColor', $attrs['isSynced'] ) ) {\n  $item_style .= 'background-color: var(--primary-color);';\n}\n```\n\n**3. Per-Block CSS Class Architecture**\n- Each block has dedicated CSS class extending Base_CSS\n- Isolated concerns: Accordion_CSS handles only accordion styling\n- Auto-discovered and loaded via autoload_block_classes()\n- Highly maintainable and scalable\n\n**4. Dynamic Content Regex System**\n- Custom HTML tags `<o-dynamic>` and magic tags `{otterDynamic?...}` \n- Regex-based parsing (though author notes: \"Todo: Improve this Regex, it can't go on for like this. Soon it will be longer than the available space in the universe!!!\")\n- Decouples dynamic content from core block rendering\n\n**5. Block Conditions as Render Filter**\n- Single `otterConditions` attribute added to ALL blocks\n- Evaluated via `render_block` filter at priority 999\n- Completely transparent to block developers\n- Condition collections: OR groups AND conditions (elegant boolean algebra)\n\n**6. Atomic Wind Experimental System**\n- Minimal \"atomic\" primitive blocks (box, text, icon, image, link)\n- Tailwind CSS generation pipeline\n- Cached CSS output per post\n- Query loop rendering with field substitution\n- Animation and state system for advanced interactions\n\nOpt-in via setting: `themeisle_blocks_settings_atomic_wind_blocks`\n\n**7. Responsive Design Pattern**\n- Consistent Desktop/Tablet/Mobile attribute naming\n- Unified across 47 blocks\n- CSS variable approach allows media-query-free styling in some cases\n\n**8. Form Provider Interface**\nInterface: `/inc/integrations/interfaces/interface-form-subscribe-service.php`\n\n- Abstraction for multiple email providers (Mailchimp, Sendinblue)\n- Easy to add new providers without modifying core form block\n- Settings stored in wp_options via WP Fusion\n\n**9. Block Pattern Categories**\n- 12 themed categories (Business, Fitness, Creator, Recipes, etc.)\n- Helps organize 60+ patterns\n- Each pattern versioned with minimum WP version\n\n**10. AMP & Performance Optimizations**\n- Animation scripts loaded conditionally\n- Widgets CSS enqueued only when needed\n- Fonts fetched per-post (post_meta driven)\n- CSS minification via `tubalmartin\\CssMin\\Minifier`\n- Optional object cache support\n\n---\n\n## SUMMARY STATISTICS\n\n| Category | Count |\n|----------|-------|\n| **Total Blocks** | 47 (42 Otter + 5 Atomic Wind) |\n|
